# Web/Desktop ProductClient move ledger

Authoritative, checked classification of every file under `apps/desktop/src`
for the later mechanical move into `@proliferate/product-client`
([[Move the Desktop Product into ProductClient]]). This PR (Prove ProductClient
Extraction Mechanics) produces and checks the ledger; **it moves nothing**.

- Base SHA: **f93afce8190bba943277d588c9bfb0d051c615c9** (`origin/main`; slices
  01/02 merged as #1180/#1182).
- Source root: `apps/desktop/src` (2220 files at base).
- Checker: `scripts/check-product-client-move-ledger.py` parses the `ledger`
  block below.

## Classification vocabulary

- `move` — product module; relocates verbatim to
  `apps/packages/product-client/src/<same relative path>`. Its Desktop-local
  `@/` imports of other moved modules become `#product/*` at the codemod stage.
- `split` — the file has a host responsibility that must stay behind (or needs a
  new host port) **and** a product part that moves; the reason names the concrete
  host part, and the target is the product part's destination.
- `retain` — Desktop host module; stays in `apps/desktop/src` (no target).
- `delete` — provably dead; removed by the move PR (no target).

## Binding rules

Default is `move` to `apps/packages/product-client/src/<relpath>`. `retain`
covers exactly these host buckets (per merged slices 01/02 and the
architecture doc):

- `main.tsx`;
  `providers/DesktopHostProviders.tsx`(+test);
  `providers/DesktopProductHostProvider.tsx`(+test);
  `providers/desktop-product-host.ts`(+test); `providers/app-query-client.ts`
- `lib/access/tauri/**`; `lib/integrations/telemetry/**`;
  `lib/integrations/auth/**`; `lib/infra/measurement/**`;
  `hooks/access/tauri/**`
- `stores/auth/auth-store.ts`;
  `hooks/auth/workflows/use-auth-actions.ts`;
  `hooks/auth/workflows/use-auth-orchestration-effects.ts`;
  `hooks/auth/lifecycle/use-auth-bootstrap.ts`
- `lib/infra/proliferate-api.ts`; `lib/access/cloud/client.ts`

Tests classify with their subject.

### Audited retain exceptions (outside the named buckets, kept with evidence)

Re-read at merge time; both **directly** import `getPreferencesStore` from
`@/lib/access/tauri/store` (the raw Tauri preferences store) and therefore *are*
the Desktop implementation of the host "non-secret product persistence"
capability. Moving either would drag a `@/`/Tauri import into product-client and
fail `check_frontend_boundaries.py`, so they retain:

- `lib/access/browser/product-storage.ts`(+`.test.ts`) — `desktopProductStorage`.
- `lib/infra/persistence/preferences-persistence.ts` — `readPersistedValue`/
  `persistValue`, consumed only by retained
  `lib/access/tauri/ssh-target-profile.ts`.

## Reconciliation decisions (this merge stage)

The ledger merges two parallel classifier passes with disk ground truth. The
one substantive cross-pass disagreement was **measurement coupling**:

1. **Measurement is `move`+seam, not `split`.** One pass split every product
   file importing `lib/infra/measurement/**`; the other classified them `move`
   and deferred to this merge ("flag for L merge, not split"). Resolved to
   `move` per the `split` definition (host *responsibility* vs host
   *dependency*): `lib/infra/measurement/**` is host-retained boot diagnostics
   and is **not** a `ProductHost` capability, but an otherwise-product file that
   merely records a latency/metric has no host *responsibility* to leave behind
   — only a host *dependency* to reroute. Every such row carries a
   `measurement` seam tag; the codemod / move PR must reroute those imports
   through a host-supplied measurement facade (they cannot become `#product/*`
   because measurement stays host).
2. **`split` is reserved for genuine host work / a missing host port**: raw
   Tauri ops (`tauri/window`, the `tauri/connect-server` HTTP probe), auth
   operations not yet exposed by `ProductHost` (sign-in, SSO discovery, GitHub
   availability, auth-methods, org-join invitation flow), a bare
   `import "@/lib/access/cloud/client"` client-factory side-effect, and the
   three boundary files `App.tsx`, `assets.d.ts`,
   `providers/DesktopProductLifecycleRoot.tsx`.
3. **Reroutable host dependencies stay `move`+seam** (not split): pure host
   utilities (`isAbortError`), deployment-identity reads via
   `lib/infra/proliferate-api` (host capability *exists*), telemetry-vendor
   capture via `lib/integrations/telemetry/client` (host capability *exists*),
   and type-only host imports. Seam tags (`measurement`, `deployment-identity`,
   `cloud-client`, `telemetry`, `auth`) are derived deterministically by grep
   over `apps/desktop/src` and only applied to non-retained files.

## Known wrinkles (recorded per brief)

- **`catalog.json` `?raw` external reach.**
  `lib/domain/agents/bundled-agent-catalog.ts` imports
  `../../../../../../catalogs/agents/catalog.json?raw`, reaching six levels up to
  repo-root `catalogs/agents/catalog.json` (~246 KB), **outside** `apps/desktop`.
  Classified `move` (product), but the relative `?raw` specifier breaks on the
  directory-depth change. The move PR must re-resolve it (a build-time copy of
  `catalog.json` into the package, or a stable alias); the S1 qualification
  canary already proves an analogous `?raw` JSON reach.
- **Duplicate `product-storage.ts`.** Two distinct modules with distinct paths
  (targets do not collide): `lib/access/browser/product-storage.ts` = `retain`
  (raw-Tauri host-capability impl); `lib/infra/persistence/product-storage.ts` =
  `move` (generic `ProductStorageContext` helper, type-only host import).
- **Scratch bridge consumers.** `hooks/access/tauri/workspace-scratch/**` and
  `lib/access/tauri/workspace-scratch.ts` = `retain` (bridge consumers / raw
  store); the product side already consumes scratch via `host.desktop.scratch`,
  so no product move is needed for the bridge layer.

## Ledger

Tab-separated: `source-path<TAB>classification<TAB>target<TAB>reason`. Paths are
relative to `apps/desktop/src`; targets are repo-relative. `retain`/`delete`
rows have an empty target. This block is the machine-parseable contract consumed
by `scripts/check-product-client-move-ledger.py`; do not reformat it.

## Codemod evidence (S5)

`scripts/migrate-desktop-product-client.mjs` is the ledger-driven import codemod.
It reads this ledger with the same parse semantics as
`scripts/check-product-client-move-ledger.py` (fenced ` ```ledger ` block,
tab-split rows, >=4 fields, valid classification) and, for every `move`-classified
JS/TS module, rewrites Desktop-local specifiers (`@/...` alias and relative
`./`,`../`) that resolve to another `move`-classified JS/TS module into
package-private `#product/*` specifiers. Specifier string-literal nodes are located
with the TypeScript parser and spliced by position; no fallback text replacement.

Scope (justified): the package `imports` map resolves `#product/*` only to
`./dist/*.js`, so only compiled JS/TS modules are eligible. Local specifiers that
resolve to a `retain`/`split`/`delete` target, to an **asset/CSS/JSON** file
(e.g. `@/assets/...svg?raw`), or **outside** `apps/desktop/src` (the six-level
`catalogs/agents/catalog.json?raw` reach) are left untouched — a co-moved relative
asset import stays valid after the move, and an aliased asset/external import
cannot be expressed as `#product/*`. Those are the move-PR asset-resolution items
already recorded under "Known wrinkles". Seam imports (e.g. product files reading
`lib/infra/measurement/**`) resolve to `retain` rows and are therefore correctly
left as `@/...` here, to be rerouted through host facades by the move PR.

Proof on a disposable copy of `apps/desktop/src` (real working tree never written):

- `--check`  -> 5653 planned rewrites across 1601 files (1985 move modules scanned).
- `--apply`  -> 5653 applied; plan byte-identical to `--check`.
- `--check` after apply -> 0 (empty).
- `--apply` second run -> 0 (idempotent).
- Two independent full `--apply` runs produce byte-identical trees (deterministic;
  stable sort by source path then in-file position, no timestamps).
- Applied diffs touch only import/export specifier tokens (file line counts
  preserved; every rewritten specifier is `#product/*`).
- Refuses (exit nonzero) on: a 3-field row, an unterminated ` ```ledger ` block, an
  unknown classification, a `move` source importing a path with no ledger row, and a
  missing `--check`/`--apply` mode.

Run against a copy, not the working source:

```bash
cp -R apps/desktop/src /tmp/proof-src
node scripts/migrate-desktop-product-client.mjs --check --src /tmp/proof-src
node scripts/migrate-desktop-product-client.mjs --apply --src /tmp/proof-src
node scripts/migrate-desktop-product-client.mjs --check --src /tmp/proof-src   # empty
```
